function fmt(d?: string | null) {
  if (!d) return '—';
  try { return format(new Date(d), 'dd MMM yyyy HH:mm', { locale: ar }); } catch { return d; }
}

const STATUS_CFG: Record<string, { label: string; cls: string }> = {
  active:    { label: 'نشط',    cls: 'bg-success/10 text-success border-success/20' },
  suspended: { label: 'موقوف', cls: 'bg-warning/10 text-warning border-warning/20' },
  disabled:  { label: 'معطل',  cls: 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground border-border' },
  blocked:   { label: 'محظور', cls: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive border-destructive/20' },
  deleted:   { label: 'محذوف', cls: 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive border-destructive/20' },
};

function MerchantStatusBadge({ status }: { status: string }) {
  const cfg = STATUS_CFG[status] ?? STATUS_CFG.active;
  return (
    <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full border text-[10px] font-semibold ${cfg.cls}`}>
      <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-current inline-block" />
      {cfg.label}
    </span>
  );
}

function StatCard({ icon: Icon, label, value, color = '' }: {
  icon: React.ElementType; label: string; value: React.ReactNode; color?: string;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 rounded-2xl border border-border bg-card p-4 text-center">
      <div className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center mb-1 ${color || 'bg-primary/10'}`}>
        <Icon className={`w-4 h-4 ${color ? '' : 'text-primary'}`} />
      </div>
      <p className="text-lg font-black tabular-nums">{value}</p>
      <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{label}</p>
    </div>
  );
}

/** تحويل تاجر إلى مستخدم عادي (يؤرشف البيانات، لا يحذف) */
export async function demoteToUser(
  userId: string,
  adminId?: string
): Promise<{ success: boolean; merchant_id?: string; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('demote_to_user', {
    p_user_id:  userId,
    p_admin_id: adminId ?? null,
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, error: error.message };
  const result = data as { success: boolean; merchant_id?: string; error?: string };
  return result;
}

/** تحويل تاجر إلى مستخدم عادي (يحتفظ ببيانات المتجر، لا يحذف) */
export async function demoteToUser(
  userId: string,
  adminId?: string
): Promise<{ success: boolean; merchant_id?: string; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.rpc('demote_from_merchant', {
    p_user_id:  userId,
    p_admin_id: adminId ?? null,
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, error: error.message };
  const result = data as { success: boolean; merchant_id?: string; error?: string };
  return result;
}
```

    if (action === 'check_device_ban') {
      const { device_fp, device_id, hardware_hash } = body as Record<string, string | undefined>;
      if (!device_fp && !device_id && !hardware_hash) return json({ banned: false });

      let query = supabaseAdmin.from('device_bans')
        .select('id, ban_reason, banned_at').eq('is_active', true);

      const orParts: string[] = [];
      if (device_fp)     orParts.push(`device_fp.eq.${device_fp}`);

      if (hardware_hash) orParts.push(`hardware_hash.eq.${hardware_hash}`);
      if (orParts.length > 1) query = query.or(orParts.join(','));
      else if (device_fp)     query = query.eq('device_fp', device_fp);
      else if (device_id)     query = query.eq('device_id', device_id);
      else                    query = query.eq('hardware_hash', hardware_hash!);

      const { data: banRows } = await query.limit(1);
      if (banRows?.length) {
        const b = banRows[0] as { ban_reason: string; banned_at: string };
        return json({ banned: true, reason: b.ban_reason, banned_at: b.banned_at });
      }
      return json({ banned: false });
    }

    if (action === 'register_device') {
      if (!userId) return json({ error: 'userId مطلوب' }, 400);

        user_id: userId, device_fp: device_fp ?? null, device_id: device_id ?? null,

        device_model: device_model ?? null, platform: platform ?? null,
        app_version: app_version ?? null, last_seen_at: new Date().toISOString(),
      }, { onConflict: 'user_id,device_fp', ignoreDuplicates: false }).catch(() => {});
      return json({ success: true });

    if (action === 'get_device_bans') {
      const { data: bans, error: bErr } = await supabaseAdmin
        .from('device_bans').select('*').order('banned_at', { ascending: false }).limit(200);
      if (bErr) return json({ error: bErr.message }, 500);
      return json({ success: true, data: bans ?? [] });
    }

    return json({ error: `إجراء غير معروف: ${action}` }, 400);

  } catch (err) {
    return json({ error: String(err) }, 500);
  }
});

// ============================================================
// بصمة الجهاز — UUID ثابت لكل جهاز/تثبيت
// يُخزَّن في localStorage ويبقى عبر تبديل الحسابات
// يُستخدم لمنع تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز للاستفادة
// من كودَي الهدية والتجريبي أكثر من مرة
// ============================================================

const FP_KEY = '__vfp_dfp';

/**
 * يُعيد بصمة UUID ثابتة للجهاز الحالي.
 * تُولَّد مرة واحدة وتُحفظ في localStorage إلى الأبد.
 */
export function getDeviceFingerprint(): string {
  try {
    const existing = localStorage.getItem(FP_KEY);
    if (existing && existing.length === 36) return existing;

    const fp = generateUUID();
    localStorage.setItem(FP_KEY, fp);
    return fp;
  } catch {
    // في حالة حظر localStorage (نادر جداً في WebView)
    return generateUUID();
  }
}

function generateUUID(): string {
  if (typeof crypto !== 'undefined' && crypto.randomUUID) {
    return crypto.randomUUID();
  }
  // Polyfill للإصدارات القديمة من WebView
  return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, (c) => {
    const r = (Math.random() * 16) | 0;
    const v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3) | 0x8;
    return v.toString(16);
  });
}

New String: ```
// ============================================================
// بصمة الجهاز — متعددة الإشارات ومقاومة للحذف وإعادة التثبيت
// الإشارات المستخدمة:
//   1. localStorage UUID (أسرع وأبسط)
//   2. hardware_hash: مشتق من خصائص الجهاز الثابتة (Canvas/WebGL/Screen/CPU)
//   3. device_id: يُرسَل من Android Native عبر header/window
// ============================================================

const FP_KEY     = '__vfp_dfp';
const HW_KEY     = '__vfp_hwfp';
const STABLE_KEY = '__vfp_stable'; // يدمج localStorage + hardware للاستمرارية

// ── استخراج device_id من Android Native ──────────────────────────────
export function getNativeDeviceId(): string | null {
  try {
    // Capacitor يحقن الـ device_id في window.__DEVICE_ID__ عبر capacitor.config
    // أو يمكن قراءته من cookie محقون أو localStorage من Native
    const w = window as Window & { __DEVICE_ID__?: string; __ANDROID_ID__?: string };
    return w.__DEVICE_ID__ ?? w.__ANDROID_ID__ ?? localStorage.getItem('__vfp_native_id');
  } catch { return null; }
}

// ── حساب hardware_hash من خصائص الجهاز الثابتة ───────────────────────
export function computeHardwareHash(): string {
  try {
    const parts: string[] = [];

    // 1. Screen resolution + color depth
    parts.push(`${screen.width}x${screen.height}x${screen.colorDepth}`);

    // 2. Timezone
    parts.push(Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone);

    // 3. Language
    parts.push(navigator.language);

    // 4. CPU cores
    parts.push(String(navigator.hardwareConcurrency ?? 0));

    // 5. Platform (OS)
    parts.push(navigator.platform ?? '');

    // 6. User-Agent hash (أول 80 حرف)
    parts.push((navigator.userAgent ?? '').slice(0, 80));

    // 7. Canvas fingerprint
    try {
      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
      if (ctx) {
        ctx.textBaseline = 'top';
        ctx.font = '14px Arial';
        ctx.fillText('VFP🔒بصمة', 2, 2);
        ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(200,0,100,0.5)';
        ctx.fillRect(10, 10, 100, 20);
        parts.push(canvas.toDataURL().slice(-50));
      }
    } catch { /* ignore */ }

    // 8. WebGL renderer
    try {
      const gl = document.createElement('canvas').getContext('webgl');
      if (gl) {
        const dbgInfo = gl.getExtension('WEBGL_debug_renderer_info');
        if (dbgInfo) {
          parts.push(gl.getParameter(dbgInfo.UNMASKED_RENDERER_WEBGL) ?? '');
          parts.push(gl.getParameter(dbgInfo.UNMASKED_VENDOR_WEBGL) ?? '');
        }
      }
    } catch { /* ignore */ }

    // تحويل للـ hash باستخدام djb2
    const raw = parts.join('|');
    let h = 5381;
    for (let i = 0; i < raw.length; i++) {
      h = ((h << 5) + h) ^ raw.charCodeAt(i);
      h = h >>> 0;
    }
    return h.toString(16).padStart(8, '0');
  } catch {
    return 'hw-fallback';
  }
}

// ── الدالة الرئيسية: بصمة UUID ثابتة (localStorage) ─────────────────
export function getDeviceFingerprint(): string {
  try {
    const existing = localStorage.getItem(FP_KEY);
    if (existing && existing.length === 36) return existing;
    const fp = generateUUID();
    localStorage.setItem(FP_KEY, fp);
    return fp;
  } catch {
    return generateUUID();
  }
}

// ── hardware hash مع cache ────────────────────────────────────────────
export function getHardwareHash(): string {
  try {
    const cached = localStorage.getItem(HW_KEY);
    if (cached && cached.length >= 6) return cached;
    const hw = computeHardwareHash();
    localStorage.setItem(HW_KEY, hw);
    return hw;
  } catch {
    return computeHardwareHash();
  }
}

// ── بصمة مستقرة تجمع localStorage + hardware ─────────────────────────
// تعيش حتى لو حُذف localStorage — يمكن إعادة استنتاجها من hardware
export function getStableDeviceIdentity(): {
  device_fp: string;
  hardware_hash: string;
  device_id: string | null;
} {
  const device_fp    = getDeviceFingerprint();
  const hardware_hash = getHardwareHash();
  const device_id    = getNativeDeviceId();

  // إذا فُقد device_fp من localStorage ولكن hardware_hash موجود — نسجّل مرة أخرى
  try {
    const stableFp = localStorage.getItem(STABLE_KEY);
    if (!stableFp) {
      // أول مرة: احفظ الـ hardware_hash كمرجع للتعرف المستقبلي
      localStorage.setItem(STABLE_KEY, `${device_fp}:${hardware_hash}`);
    }
  } catch { /* ignore */ }

  return { device_fp, hardware_hash, device_id };
}

function generateUUID(): string {
  if (typeof crypto !== 'undefined' && crypto.randomUUID) return crypto.randomUUID();
  return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, (c) => {
    const r = (Math.random() * 16) | 0;
    return (c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3) | 0x8).toString(16);
  });
}

```
// شاشة حظر الجهاز — تظهر عند محاولة تسجيل الدخول أو إنشاء حساب من جهاز محظور
import { ShieldX, Phone } from 'lucide-react';

interface Props {
  reason?: string;
  bannedAt?: string;
}

export default function DeviceBannedScreen({ reason, bannedAt }: Props) {
  const formatDate = (d?: string) => {
    if (!d) return '';
    try {
      return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('ar-EG', {
        year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric',
      });
    } catch { return d; }
  };

  return (
    <div
      dir="rtl"
      className="min-h-screen bg-black flex flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 text-white"
    >
      {/* أيقونة الحظر */}
      <div className="w-24 h-24 rounded-full bg-destructive/10 border-2 border-destructive/30 flex items-center justify-center mb-6">
        <ShieldX className="w-12 h-12 text-destructive" />
      </div>

      {/* العنوان */}
      <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-destructive mb-2 text-center">
        تم حظر هذا الجهاز
      </h1>
      <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center mb-6 max-w-xs leading-relaxed">
        لا يمكن استخدام تطبيق Vodafone Fakka من هذا الجهاز.
        لن تتمكن من تسجيل الدخول أو إنشاء حساب جديد.
      </p>

      {/* سبب الحظر */}
      {reason && (
        <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/20 rounded-xl p-4 mb-4 text-right">
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">سبب الحظر</p>
          <p className="text-sm font-medium text-foreground">{reason}</p>
          {bannedAt && (
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-2">
              تاريخ الحظر: {formatDate(bannedAt)}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* معلومات التواصل */}
      <div className="w-full max-w-sm bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-4 text-right">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
          <Phone className="w-4 h-4 text-primary shrink-0" />
          <p className="text-sm font-semibold">هل تعتقد أن هذا خطأ؟</p>
        </div>
        <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
          إذا كنت تعتقد أن هذا الحظر تم بالخطأ، تواصل مع الدعم الفني عبر المسؤول المباشر وأعطه معرّف جهازك.
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* كود خطأ صغير في الأسفل */}
      <p className="mt-8 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/40 font-mono">
        ERR_DEVICE_BANNED
      </p>
    </div>
  );
}

/** جلب تفاصيل تاجر واحد: أعضاء + عمليات + نقاط + اشتراكات + أكواد + logs */
export async function adminGetMerchantDetail(merchantId: string): Promise<{
  merchant:      MerchantFull | null;
  members:       MerchantMember[];
  operations:    unknown[];
  subscriptions: unknown[];
  codes:         unknown[];
}> {
  const [mRes, mmRes, opsRes, subsRes, codesRes] = await Promise.all([
    supabase.from('merchants').select('*').eq('id', merchantId).single(),
    supabase.from('merchant_members')
      .select('*, profiles(username, email, phone, avatar_url)')
      .eq('merchant_id', merchantId)
      .order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
    supabase.from('merchant_operations')
      .select('*').eq('merchant_id', merchantId).order('created_at', { ascending: false }).limit(200),
    supabase.from('merchant_member_subscriptions')
      .select('*').eq('merchant_id', merchantId).order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
    supabase.from('merchant_license_codes')
      .select('*').eq('merchant_id', merchantId).order('created_at', { ascending: false }),
  ]);
  return {
    merchant:      mRes.data as MerchantFull | null,
    members:       Array.isArray(mmRes.data) ? mmRes.data : [],
    operations:    Array.isArray(opsRes.data) ? opsRes.data : [],
    subscriptions: Array.isArray(subsRes.data) ? subsRes.data : [],
    codes:         Array.isArray(codesRes.data) ? codesRes.data : [],
  };
}

// ══ نظام حظر الأجهزة وكشف الحسابات المكررة ══════════════════════════════

export interface DeviceBan {
  id: string;
  device_fp: string | null;
  device_id: string | null;
  hardware_hash: string | null;
  ban_reason: string;
  ban_type: string;
  is_permanent: boolean;
  is_active: boolean;
  associated_user_ids: string[];
  associated_usernames: string[];
  banned_by: string | null;
  banned_by_name: string | null;
  banned_at: string;
  unbanned_at: string | null;
  notes: string | null;
  ip_address: string | null;
  device_model: string | null;
  platform: string | null;
}

export interface DuplicateDeviceGroup {
  device_fp: string | null;
  device_id: string | null;
  hardware_hash: string | null;
  user_count: number;
  user_ids: string[];
  usernames: string[];
  phones: string[];
  first_seen: string;
  last_seen: string;
  is_banned: boolean;
  ban_info: Partial<DeviceBan> | null;
}

/** حظر جهاز نهائياً */
export async function banDevice(params: {
  device_fp?: string; device_id?: string; hardware_hash?: string;
  ban_reason?: string; ban_type?: string; notes?: string;
  ip_address?: string; device_model?: string; platform?: string;
  associated_user_ids?: string[]; associated_usernames?: string[];
}): Promise<{ success: boolean; ban_id?: string; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'ban_device', ...params },
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, error: error.message };
  return data as { success: boolean; ban_id?: string; error?: string };
}

/** رفع حظر جهاز */
export async function unbanDevice(ban_id: string): Promise<{ success: boolean; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'unban_device', ban_id },
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, error: error.message };
  return data as { success: boolean; error?: string };
}

/** جلب الأجهزة المكررة (حسابات متعددة على نفس الجهاز) */
export async function getDuplicateDevices(): Promise<{
  success: boolean; data: DuplicateDeviceGroup[]; total: number; error?: string;
}> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'get_duplicate_devices' },
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, data: [], total: 0, error: error.message };
  return data as { success: boolean; data: DuplicateDeviceGroup[]; total: number };
}

/** جلب قائمة حظر الأجهزة */
export async function getDeviceBans(): Promise<{ success: boolean; data: DeviceBan[]; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'get_device_bans' },
  });
  if (error) return { success: false, data: [], error: error.message };
  return data as { success: boolean; data: DeviceBan[] };
}

/** فحص حظر الجهاز الحالي — يُستدعى عند فتح التطبيق */
export async function checkDeviceBan(params: {
  device_fp?: string; device_id?: string; hardware_hash?: string;
}): Promise<{ banned: boolean; reason?: string; banned_at?: string; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'check_device_ban', ...params },
  });
  if (error) return { banned: false, error: error.message };
  return data as { banned: boolean; reason?: string; banned_at?: string };
}

/** تسجيل جهاز في registry */
export async function registerDeviceInRegistry(userId: string, params: {
  device_fp?: string; device_id?: string; hardware_hash?: string;
  ip_address?: string; device_model?: string; platform?: string; app_version?: string;
}): Promise<void> {
  await supabase.functions.invoke('admin-user-actions', {
    body: { action: 'register_device', userId, ...params },
  }).catch(() => {});
}

// صفحة إدارة الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import {
  Smartphone, ShieldX, ShieldCheck, RefreshCw, Loader2,
  Users, AlertTriangle, ChevronDown, ChevronUp, Trash2,
  Eye, Ban, CheckCircle, Clock, Info, Search, Filter,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Badge } from '@/components/ui/badge';
import { Tabs, TabsContent, TabsList, TabsTrigger } from '@/components/ui/tabs';
import AdminShell, { SectionCard, ConfirmDialog } from '@/components/admin/AdminShell';
import {
  getDuplicateDevices, getDeviceBans, banDevice, unbanDevice,
  type DuplicateDeviceGroup, type DeviceBan,
} from '@/lib/api';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { format } from 'date-fns';
import { ar } from 'date-fns/locale';

function fmt(d?: string | null) {
  if (!d) return '—';
  try { return format(new Date(d), 'dd MMM yyyy HH:mm', { locale: ar }); }
  catch { return d; }
}

function shortFp(fp?: string | null) {
  if (!fp) return '—';
  return fp.length > 12 ? `${fp.slice(0, 6)}…${fp.slice(-6)}` : fp;
}

// ── بطاقة مجموعة أجهزة مكررة ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function DuplicateGroupCard({
  group, onBan,
}: { group: DuplicateDeviceGroup; onBan: (g: DuplicateDeviceGroup) => void }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-xl border bg-card transition-all ${group.is_banned ? 'border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/3' : 'border-border'}`}>
      {/* رأس البطاقة */}
      <button
        className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right"
        onClick={() => setExpanded(v => !v)}
      >
        <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${group.is_banned ? 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive' : 'bg-warning/10 text-warning'}`}>
          {group.is_banned ? <ShieldX className="w-5 h-5" /> : <AlertTriangle className="w-5 h-5" />}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold">
              {group.user_count} حسابات على نفس الجهاز
            </span>
            {group.is_banned && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[10px]">محظور</Badge>
            )}
          </div>
          <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground font-mono mt-0.5 truncate">
            FP: {shortFp(group.device_fp)}
            {group.device_id ? ` · ID: ${shortFp(group.device_id)}` : ''}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{fmt(group.last_seen)}</span>
          {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />}
        </div>
      </button>

      {/* تفاصيل موسّعة */}
      {expanded && (
        <div className="border-t border-border px-4 pb-4 pt-3 space-y-3">
          {/* معرفات الجهاز */}
          <div className="bg-muted/40 rounded-lg p-3 space-y-1.5 text-xs font-mono">
            {group.device_fp && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_fp: </span>{group.device_fp}</p>
            )}
            {group.device_id && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_id: </span>{group.device_id}</p>
            )}
            {group.hardware_hash && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">hw_hash: </span>{group.hardware_hash}</p>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* الحسابات المرتبطة */}
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
              <Users className="w-3 h-3" /> الحسابات المرتبطة ({group.user_count})
            </p>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              {group.usernames.map((name, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="flex items-center justify-between bg-muted/30 rounded-lg px-3 py-2">
                  <span className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">{group.user_ids[i]?.slice(0, 8)}…</span>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-xs font-semibold">{name ?? '—'}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{group.phones?.[i] ?? '—'}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* معلومات الحظر الحالية */}
          {group.is_banned && group.ban_info && (
            <div className="bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/20 rounded-lg p-3">
              <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-destructive mb-1">معلومات الحظر</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">السبب: {group.ban_info.ban_reason ?? '—'}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">بواسطة: {group.ban_info.banned_by_name ?? '—'}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">تاريخ: {fmt(group.ban_info.banned_at)}</p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* الإجراءات */}
          {!group.is_banned && (
            <Button
              variant="destructive"
              size="sm"
              className="w-full gap-2"
              onClick={() => onBan(group)}
            >
              <Ban className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
              حظر هذا الجهاز نهائياً
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── بطاقة حظر جهاز في القائمة ────────────────────────────────────────────
function BanCard({ ban, onUnban }: { ban: DeviceBan; onUnban: (id: string) => void }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-xl border bg-card ${ban.is_active ? 'border-destructive/25' : 'border-border opacity-60'}`}>
      <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right" onClick={() => setExpanded(v => !v)}>
        <div className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${ban.is_active ? 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive' : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground'}`}>
          {ban.is_active ? <ShieldX className="w-4 h-4" /> : <ShieldCheck className="w-4 h-4" />}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold">{ban.ban_reason}</span>
            <Badge variant={ban.is_active ? 'destructive' : 'secondary'} className="text-[10px]">
              {ban.is_active ? 'نشط' : 'مرفوع'}
            </Badge>
          </div>
          <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground font-mono truncate">
            {shortFp(ban.device_fp)}{ban.device_id ? ` · ${shortFp(ban.device_id)}` : ''}
          </p>
        </div>
        <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground shrink-0">{fmt(ban.banned_at)}</span>
      </button>

      {expanded && (
        <div className="border-t border-border px-4 pb-4 pt-3 space-y-2.5">
          <div className="bg-muted/40 rounded-lg p-3 text-xs font-mono space-y-1">
            {ban.device_fp  && <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_fp: </span>{ban.device_fp}</p>}
            {ban.device_id  && <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_id: </span>{ban.device_id}</p>}
            {ban.hardware_hash && <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">hw_hash: </span>{ban.hardware_hash}</p>}
            {ban.ip_address && <p><span className="text-muted-foreground">IP: </span>{ban.ip_address}</p>}
            {ban.device_model && <p><span className="text-muted-foreground">الجهاز: </span>{ban.device_model}</p>}
          </div>
          {ban.associated_usernames?.length > 0 && (
            <div>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1">الحسابات المرتبطة:</p>
              <p className="text-xs font-semibold">{ban.associated_usernames.join(' · ')}</p>
            </div>
          )}
          {ban.notes && (
            <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground flex gap-1 items-start">
              <Info className="w-3 h-3 shrink-0 mt-0.5" />{ban.notes}
            </p>
          )}
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            <Clock className="w-3 h-3" />
            <span>بواسطة: {ban.banned_by_name ?? '—'} · {fmt(ban.banned_at)}</span>
          </div>
          {ban.is_active && (
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="w-full gap-2" onClick={() => onUnban(ban.id)}>
              <ShieldCheck className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
              رفع الحظر
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── الصفحة الرئيسية ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'bans'>('duplicates');

  const [dupes, setDupes]       = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
  const [bans,  setBans]        = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading]   = useState(true);
  const [search, setSearch]     = useState('');
  const [filterBanned, setFilterBanned] = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');

  // حوار الحظر
  const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
  const [banNote, setBanNote]     = useState('');
  const [banning, setBanning]     = useState(false);

  // حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر
  const [unbanId, setUnbanId]   = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [unbanning, setUnbanning] = useState(false);

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [d, b] = await Promise.all([getDuplicateDevices(), getDeviceBans()]);
      if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
      else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
      if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  // تصفية الأجهزة المكررة
  const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    const matchQ = !q ||
      (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
      g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
    const matchFilter =
      filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
      filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned :
      !g.is_banned;
    return matchQ && matchFilter;
  });

  // تصفية قائمة الحظر
  const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q ||
      (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  });

  const handleBan = async () => {
    if (!banTarget) return;
    setBanning(true);
    const res = await banDevice({
      device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
      device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
      hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,
      ban_reason:           banNote.trim() || 'تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز',
      ban_type:             'both',
      notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
      associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
      associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,
    });
    setBanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم حظر الجهاز نهائياً');
      setBanTarget(null);
      setBanNote('');
      await load();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');
    }
  };

  const handleUnban = async () => {
    if (!unbanId) return;
    setUnbanning(true);
    const res = await unbanDevice(unbanId);
    setUnbanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
      setUnbanId(null);
      await load();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');
    }
  };

  const activeBansCount = bans.filter(b => b.is_active).length;

  return (
    <AdminShell title="الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة" onBack={() => navigate('/admin')}>
      {/* إحصائيات سريعة */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 mb-4">
        {[
          { label: 'أجهزة مكررة', value: dupes.length, icon: Smartphone, color: 'text-warning' },
          { label: 'محظور منهم', value: dupes.filter(d => d.is_banned).length, icon: ShieldX, color: 'text-destructive' },
          { label: 'حظر نشط', value: activeBansCount, icon: Ban, color: 'text-destructive' },
        ].map(({ label, value, icon: Icon, color }) => (
          <div key={label} className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-3 text-center">
            <Icon className={`w-5 h-5 mx-auto mb-1 ${color}`} />
            <p className="text-lg font-bold tabular-nums">{loading ? '—' : value}</p>
            <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* شريط البحث + تحديث */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
        <div className="relative flex-1">
          <Search className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
          <Input
            placeholder="ابحث بالاسم أو الجهاز أو الهاتف…"
            value={search}
            onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)}
            className="pr-9 text-sm h-9"
            dir="rtl"
          />
        </div>
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={load} disabled={loading} className="shrink-0">
          {loading ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4" />}
        </Button>
      </div>

      <Tabs value={tab} onValueChange={v => setTab(v as typeof tab)}>
        <TabsList className="w-full mb-4">
          <TabsTrigger value="duplicates" className="flex-1 gap-1.5 text-xs">
            <AlertTriangle className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
            أجهزة مكررة
            {dupes.length > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0">{dupes.length}</Badge>
            )}
          </TabsTrigger>
          <TabsTrigger value="bans" className="flex-1 gap-1.5 text-xs">
            <ShieldX className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
            قائمة الحظر
            {activeBansCount > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0">{activeBansCount}</Badge>
            )}
          </TabsTrigger>
        </TabsList>

        {/* تبويب الأجهزة المكررة */}
        <TabsContent value="duplicates" className="space-y-3 mt-0">
          {/* فلتر سريع */}
          <div className="flex gap-2">
            {([['all', 'الكل'], ['unbanned', 'غير محظور'], ['banned', 'محظور']] as const).map(([v, l]) => (
              <button key={v}
                onClick={() => setFilterBanned(v)}
                className={`text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full border transition-colors ${filterBanned === v ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-primary' : 'bg-card border-border text-muted-foreground'}`}
              >{l}</button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {loading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ) : filteredDupes.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
              <CheckCircle className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 text-green-500/60" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">لا توجد أجهزة مكررة</p>
              <p className="text-xs mt-1">كل الحسابات تستخدم أجهزة مختلفة</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            filteredDupes.map((g, i) => (
              <DuplicateGroupCard
                key={g.device_fp ?? g.device_id ?? i}
                group={g}
                onBan={setBanTarget}
              />
            ))
          )}
        </TabsContent>

        {/* تبويب قائمة الحظر */}
        <TabsContent value="bans" className="space-y-3 mt-0">
          {loading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ) : filteredBans.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
              <ShieldCheck className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 text-green-500/60" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">قائمة الحظر فارغة</p>
              <p className="text-xs mt-1">لم يتم حظر أي جهاز بعد</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            filteredBans.map(b => (
              <BanCard key={b.id} ban={b} onUnban={setUnbanId} />
            ))
          )}
        </TabsContent>
      </Tabs>

      {/* حوار تأكيد الحظر */}
      {banTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-50 flex items-end md:items-center justify-center p-4" dir="rtl">
          <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-2xl w-full max-w-sm p-5 space-y-4">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-destructive/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                <Ban className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <h3 className="font-bold text-sm">حظر الجهاز نهائياً</h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  {banTarget.user_count} حسابات · {shortFp(banTarget.device_fp)}
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/15 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
              ⚠️ سيُمنع الجهاز من تسجيل الدخول أو إنشاء حسابات جديدة حتى لو حذف التطبيق أو مسح البيانات.
            </div>

            <div>
              <p className="text-xs font-medium mb-1.5">سبب الحظر (اختياري)</p>
              <Input
                placeholder="مثال: إنشاء حسابات متعددة للاستفادة من العروض"
                value={banNote}
                onChange={e => setBanNote(e.target.value)}
                className="text-sm"
                dir="rtl"
              />
            </div>

            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <Button
                variant="destructive"
                className="flex-1 gap-2"
                onClick={handleBan}
                disabled={banning}
              >
                {banning ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Ban className="w-4 h-4" />}
                تأكيد الحظر
              </Button>
              <Button variant="outline" className="flex-1" onClick={() => setBanTarget(null)} disabled={banning}>
                إلغاء
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر */}
      <ConfirmDialog
        open={!!unbanId}
        title="رفع حظر الجهاز"
        desc="هل تريد رفع الحظر عن هذا الجهاز؟ سيتمكن المستخدم من تسجيل الدخول مجدداً."
        variant="default"
        action={handleUnban}
        onClose={() => setUnbanId(null)}
      />
    </AdminShell>
  );
}

```

   161

   329   const flushQueue = useCallback(async () => {
   330     if (!user) return;
   331     try {
   332       const raw = localStorage.getItem('pending_ops_queue');
   333       if (!raw) return;
   334       const queue: unknown[] = JSON.parse(raw);
   335       if (!queue.length) return;
   336       const remaining: unknown[] = [];
   337       for (const op of queue) {
   338         try {
   339           const { error } = await insertOperation(op as Parameters<typeof insertOperation>[0]);
   340           if (error) remaining.push(op);
   341         } catch { remaining.push(op); }
   342       }
   343       if (remaining.length < queue.length) {
   344         const flushed = queue.length - remaining.length;
   345         toast.success(`✅ تم تسجيل ${flushed} عملية${flushed > 1 ? ' معلّقة' : ' معلّقة'} بنجاح`);
   346       }
   347       if (remaining.length === 0) localStorage.removeItem('pending_ops_queue');
   348       else localStorage.setItem('pending_ops_queue', JSON.stringify(remaining));
   349     } catch { /* لا يوقف التطبيق */ }
   350   }, [user]);
   351 
   352   useEffect(() => {
   353     // محاولة عند فتح التطبيق مباشرة
   354     flushQueue();
   355     // محاولة عند عودة الإنترنت
   356     window.addEventListener('online', flushQueue);
   357     return () => window.removeEventListener('online', flushQueue);
   358   }, [flushQueue]);
   359 
   360   return (
   361     <>
   362       {/* MaintenanceScreen — يغطي التطبيق بالكامل فوراً من لوحة الإدارة */}
   363       {flags.ff_maintenance_mode && <MaintenanceScreen />}
   364 
   365       {/* SessionConflictScreen — الحساب مفتوح على جهاز آخر */}
   366       {!flags.ff_maintenance_mode && sessionConflict && <SessionConflictScreen />}
   367 
   368       {/* ForceUpdateScreen — يغطي كل شيء ولا يسمح بالدخول حتى التحديث */}
   369       {!flags.ff_maintenance_mode && !sessionConflict && forceUpdate && (
   370         <ForceUpdateScreen
   371           apkUrl={latestVersion?.apk_url}
   372           latestVersion={latestVersion?.version}
   373         />
   374       )}
   375 
   376       {/* SplashOverlay خارج كل Route — إضافة حاجز أخطاء محلي يمنع كراش Sentry */}
   377       {showSplash && (
   378         <PageErrorBoundary pageName="splash-overlay">
   379           <SplashOverlay onDone={handleSplashDone} />
   380         </PageErrorBoundary>

New String: ```
function AppInner() {
  const { sessionConflict } = useAuth();

  // isColdStart: true فقط إذا لم يكن للتطبيق نشاط حديث (خلال 30 دقيقة)
  const isColdStart = (() => {
    const ts = Number(localStorage.getItem(ACTIVITY_KEY) ?? 0);
    if (!ts) return true;
    return Date.now() - ts > RESUME_TTL_MS;
  })();

  const [showSplash,  setShowSplash]  = useState(isColdStart);
  const [navigateNow, setNavigateNow] = useState(!isColdStart);

  // ── فحص حظر الجهاز ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [deviceBan, setDeviceBan] = useState<{ banned: boolean; reason?: string; banned_at?: string } | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const { device_fp, hardware_hash, device_id } = getStableDeviceIdentity();
    checkDeviceBan({ device_fp, hardware_hash, device_id: device_id ?? undefined })
      .then(res => { if (res.banned) setDeviceBan(res); })
      .catch(() => {});
  }, []);
```

export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'bans'>('duplicates');

  const [dupes, setDupes]       = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
  const [bans,  setBans]        = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading]   = useState(true);
  const [search, setSearch]     = useState('');
  const [filterBanned, setFilterBanned] = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');

  // حوار الحظر
  const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
  const [banNote, setBanNote]     = useState('');
  const [banning, setBanning]     = useState(false);

  // حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر
  const [unbanId, setUnbanId]   = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [unbanning, setUnbanning] = useState(false);

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [d, b] = await Promise.all([getDuplicateDevices(), getDeviceBans()]);
      if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
      else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
      if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  // تصفية الأجهزة المكررة
  const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    const matchQ = !q ||
      (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
      g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
    const matchFilter =
      filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
      filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned :
      !g.is_banned;
    return matchQ && matchFilter;
  });

  // تصفية قائمة الحظر
  const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q ||
      (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  });

  const handleBan = async () => {
    if (!banTarget) return;
    setBanning(true);
    const res = await banDevice({
      device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
      device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
      hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,
      ban_reason:           banNote.trim() || 'تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز',
      ban_type:             'both',
      notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
      associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
      associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,
    });
    setBanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم حظر الجهاز نهائياً');
      setBanTarget(null);
      setBanNote('');
      await load();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');
    }
  };

  const handleUnban = async () => {
    if (!unbanId) return;
    setUnbanning(true);
    const res = await unbanDevice(unbanId);
    setUnbanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
      setUnbanId(null);
      await load();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');
    }
  };

  const activeBansCount = bans.filter(b => b.is_active).length;

  return (
    <AdminShell title="الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة" onBack={() => navigate('/admin')}>

export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'bans'>('duplicates');

  const [dupes, setDupes]       = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
  const [bans,  setBans]        = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading]   = useState(true);
  const [search, setSearch]     = useState('');
  const [filterBanned, setFilterBanned] = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');

  // حوار الحظر
  const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
  const [banNote, setBanNote]     = useState('');
  const [banning, setBanning]     = useState(false);

  // حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر
  const [unbanId, setUnbanId]     = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [unbanning, setUnbanning] = useState(false);

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [d, b] = await Promise.all([getDuplicateDevices(), getDeviceBans()]);
      if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
      else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
      if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    const matchQ = !q ||
      (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
      g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
    const matchFilter =
      filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
      filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned : !g.is_banned;
    return matchQ && matchFilter;
  });

  const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q ||
      (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  });

  const handleBan = async () => {
    if (!banTarget) return;
    setBanning(true);
    const res = await banDevice({
      device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
      device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
      hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,

      notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
      associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
      associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,

      setBanTarget(null);
      setBanNote('');
      await load();

      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');

      toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
      setUnbanId(null);
      await load();
    } else {
      toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');

        { label: 'الحسابات المكررة' },
      ]}
    >

Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_URL')!,\n      Deno.env.get('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY')!,\n      { auth: { autoRefreshToken: false, persistSession: false } },\n    );\n\n    const authHeader = req.headers.get('Authorization');\n    if (!authHeader) return json({ error: 'Authorization header مطلوب' }, 401);\n\n    const { data: { user: caller }, error: authErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n      .from('profiles').select('role').eq('id', caller.id).single();\n    if (!callerProfile || !['admin', 'super_admin'].includes(callerProfile.role ?? '')) {\n      return json({ error: 'يجب أن تكون أدمن لتنفيذ هذا الإجراء' }, 403);\n    }\n\n    const body = await req.json() as {\n      action: string; userId?: string; value?: unknown;\n      userIds?: string[]; title?: string; message?: string;\n    };\n    const { action, userId, value, userIds, title, message } = body;\n\n    if (!action) return json({ error: 'action مطلوب' }, 400);\n\n json({ error: 'userId مطلوب' }, 400);\n      if (userId === caller.id) return json({ error: 'لا يمكن تنفيذ هذا الإجراء على حسابك الخاص' }, 400);\n\n      const { data: targetProfile } = await supabaseAdmin\n        .from('profiles').select('id, username, email').eq('id', userId).single();\n      if (!targetProfile) return json({ error: 'المستخدم غير موجود في profiles' }, 404);\n\n      switch (action) {\n\n        case 'sign_out_all': {\n          const { error } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.signOut(userId, 'global');\n          if (error) return json({ error: `فشل تسجيل الخروج: ${error.message}` }, 500);\n          await supabaseAdmin.from('fcm_tokens')\n            .update({ is_active: false, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })\n            .eq('user_id', userId);\n          await supabaseAdmin.from('activity_log').insert({\n            user_id: userId, event_type: 'admin_sign_out_all',\n            title: 'تسجيل خروج من جميع الأجهزة',\n            description: `بواسطة الأدمن ${caller.id}`,\n          }).catch(() => {});\n          return json({ success: true, message: 'تم تسجيل الخروج من جميع الأجهزة' });\n        }\n\n        case 'reset_tokens': {\n          const { error } = await supabaseAdmin.from('fcm_tokens')\n            .update({ is_active: false, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })\n            .eq('user_id', userId);\n          if (error) return json({ error: `فشل إعادة التعيين: ${error.message}` }, 500);\n          await supabaseAdmin.from('activity_log').insert({\n            user_id: userId, event_type: 'admin_reset_device',\n            title: 'إعادة تعيين بيانات الجهاز',\n            description: `بواسطة الأدمن ${caller.id}`,\n          }).catch(() => {});\n          return json({ success: true, message: 'تم إعادة تعيين بيانات الجهاز' });\n        }\n\n        case 'set_ops_limit': {\n          const newLimit = Number(value);\n          if (isNaN(newLimit) || newLimit < 0) return json({ error: 'قيمة غير صالحة' }, 400);\n          const { error } = await supabaseAdmin.from('subscriptions')\n            .update({ ops_limit: newLimit, ops_remaining: newLimit, updated_at: new Date().toISOString() })\n            .eq('user_id', userId);\n          if (error) return json({ error: `فشل التعديل: ${error.message}` }, 500);\n          await supabaseAdmin.from('activity_log').insert({\n            user_id: userId, event_type: 'admin_set_ops_limit',\n            title: 'تعديل الحد اليومي للعمليات',\n            description: `تم تعيين الحد إلى ${newLimit} بواسطة الأدمن ${caller.id}`,\n          }).catch(() => {});\n          return json({ success: true, message: `تم تعيين الحد إلى ${newLimit} عملية` });\n        }\n\n        // ══ حذف الحساب نهائياً — مُحسَّن ══════════════════════════════\n        case 'delete_account': {\n          const errors: string[] = [];\n\n          // 1) حذف جميع الجداول المرتبطة بـ user_id (بالترتيب الآمن)\n          const relatedTables = [\n            'notification_seen',   // FK → auth.users ON DELETE CASCADE\n            'notification_deliveries', // FK → auth.users ON DELETE CASCADE\n            'notifications',       // FK → profiles ON DELETE CASCADE\n            'activity_log',        // FK → profiles ON DELETE CASCADE\n            'system_logs',         // قد لا تحتوي FK — نحذف للتنظيف\n            'favorites',           // FK → profiles\n            'operations',          // FK → profiles\n            'fcm_tokens',          // FK → profiles\n            'gift_claims',         // FK → auth.users ON DELETE CASCADE\n            'trial_usage',         // FK → profiles ON DELETE SET NULL (آمن)\n            'code_logs',           // FK → auth.users ON DELETE SET NULL\n            'device_gift_activations', // FK → auth.users ON DELETE SET NULL\n          ];\n\n          for (const table of relatedTables) {\n            const { error: tErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n              .from(table).delete().eq('user_id', userId);\n            if (tErr && !tErr.message.includes('does not exist')) {\n              console.warn(`⚠️ [delete] ${table}: ${tErr.message}`);\n              errors.push(`${table}: ${tErr.message}`);\n            }\n          }\n\n          // 2) تحرير license_keys المرتبطة بهذا المستخدم\n          const { error: lkErr } = await supabaseAdmin.from('license_keys')\n            .update({ used_by: null, بعد تحرير license_keys\n          const { error: subErr } = await supabaseAdmin.from('subscriptions')\n            .delete().eq('user_id', userId);\n          if (subErr) {\n            console.error(`❌ [delete] subscriptions: ${subErr.message}`);\n            return json({ error: `فشل حذف الاشتراكات: ${subErr.message}` }, 500);\n          }\n\n          // 4) حذف من merchants إن كان تاجراً\n          await supabaseAdmin.from('merchants').delete().eq('owner_id', userId).catch(() => {});\n\n          // 5) حذف الـ profile\n          const { error: profErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n            .from('profiles').delete().eq('id', userId);\n          if (profErr) {\n            console.error(`❌ [delete] profile: ${profErr.message}`);\n            return json({ error: `فشل حذف الملف الشخصي: ${profErr.message}` }, 500);\n          }\n\n          // 6) حذف من Auth\n          const { error: authDelErr } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.deleteUser(userId);\n          if (authDelErr) {\n            if (!authDelErr.message.includes('not found') && !authDelErr.message.includes('User not found')) {\n              console.error(`❌ [delete] auth: ${authDelErr.message}`);\n              return json({ error: `فشل حذف المستخدم من Auth: ${authDelErr.message}` }, 500);\n            }\n          }\n\n          const warn = errors.length > 0 ? ` (تحذيرات: ${errors.join(' | ')})` : '';\n          return json({ success: true, message: `تم حذف الحساب نهائياً${warn}` });\n        }\n      }\n    }\n\n    // ══ إصلاح الحسابات المفقودة (profiles بدون auth record) ══════════\n    if (action === 'repair_orphan_accounts') {\n      // جلب كل profiles\n      const { data: allProfiles, error: profErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n        .from('profiles')\n        .select('id, username, email, phone, created_at')\n        .order('created_at', { ascending: true });\n\n      if (profErr) return json({ error: `فشل جلب profiles: ${profErr.message}` }, 500);\n\n      const orphans: Array<{ id: وجوده في auth\n      for (const p of (allProfiles ?? [])) {\n        const { data: authUser, error: authErr2 } = await supabaseAdmin.auth.admin.getUserById(p.id);\n        if (authErr2 || !authUser?.user) {\n          orphans.push({ id: p.id, username: p.username, email: p.email });\n        } else {\n          valid.push({ id: p.id, username: p.username, email: p.email });\n        }\n      }\n\n      return json({\n        success: true,\n        total_profiles: allProfiles?.length ?? 0,\n        valid_accounts: valid.length,\n        orphan_count:   orphans.length,\n        orphans,\n        message: orphans.length === 0\n          ? '✅ كل الحسابات سليمة — لا يوجد حسابات مفقودة'\n          : `⚠️ وُجد ${orphans.length} حساب في profiles بدون auth record`,\n      });\n    }\n\n    // ══ إرسال إشعار لقائمة مستخدمين متضررين ════════════════════════\n    if (action === 'notify_affected_users') {\n      if (!userIds?.length) return json({ error: 'userIds مطلوب' }, 400);\n      if (!title || !message) return json({ error: 'title و message مطلوبان' }, 400);\n\n      const inserted: string[] = [];\n      const failed:   string[] = [];\n\n      for (const uid of userIds) {\n        const { error: nErr } = await supabaseAdmin.from('notifications').insert({\n          user_id:   uid,\n          title,\n          body:      message,\n          type:      'info',\n          priority:  'high',\n          is_read:   false,\n          is_global: false,\n          created_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n        });\n        if (nErr) { failed.push(uid); }\n        else       { inserted.push(uid); }\n      }\n\n      return json({\n        success: true,\n        sent:    inserted.length,\n        failed:  failed.length,\n        message: `تم إرسال الإشعار لـ ${inserted.length} مستخدم${failed.length > 0 ? ` · فشل ${failed.length}` : ''}`,\n      });\n    }\n\n    // ══ حظر جهاز نهائياً ═══════════════════════════════════════════════\n    if (action === 'ban_device') {\n      const b = body as Record<string, unknown>;\n      const { device_fp, device_id, hardware_hash, ban_reason, ban_type, notes,\n              ip_address, device_model, platform, associated_user_ids, associated_usernames } = b;\n\n      if (!device_fp && !device_id && !hardware_hash)\n        return json({ error: 'يجب توفير device_fp أو device_id على الأقل' }, 400);\n\n      const { data: callerProf } = await supabaseAdmin\n        .from('profiles').select('username').eq('id', caller.id).single();\n\n      const { data: banData, error: banErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n        .from('device_bans').insert({\n          device_fp:            device_fp ?? null,\n          ip_address:           ip_address ?? null,\n          device_model:         device_model ?? null,\n          platform:             platform ?? null,\n        }).select('id').single();\n\n      if (banErr) return json({ error: `فشل حظر الجهاز: ${banErr.message}` }, 500);\n\n      await supabaseAdmin.from('admin_audit_logs').insert({\n        action: 'ban_device', performed_by: caller.id,\n        target_user_id: (associated_user_ids as string[] | null)?.[0] ?? []).map((b: Record<string,unknown>) => b.device_fp as string).filter(Boolean));\n      const bannedIds = new Set<string>((bans ?? []).map((b: Record<string,unknown>) => b.device_id as string).filter(Boolean));\n\n      const enriched = (dupes ?? []).map((d: Record<string,unknown>) => ({\n        ...d,\n        is_banned: bannedFps.has(d.device_fp as string) || bannedIds.has(d.device_id as string),\n        ban_info: (bans ?? []).find((b: Record<string,unknown>) =>\n          (b.device_fp && b.device_fp === d.device_fp) || (b.device_id && b.device_id === d.device_id)\n        ) ?? null,\n      }));\n\n      return json({ success: true, data: enriched, total: enriched.length });\n    }\n\n    // ══ فحص حظر جهاز (يُستدعى من التطبيق عند فتحه) ═══════════════════\n    if (action === 'check_device_ban') {\n      const { device_fp, device_id, hardware_hash } = body as Record<string, string | undefined>;\n      if (!device_fp && !device_id && !hardware_hash) return json({ banned: false });\n\n      let query = supabaseAdmin.from('device_bans')\n        .select('id, ban_reason, banned_at').eq('is_active', true);\n\n      const orParts: string[] = [];\n      if (device_fp)     orParts.push(`device_fp.eq.${device_fp}`);\n      if (device_id)     orParts.push(`device_id.eq.${device_id}`);\n      if (hardware_hash) orParts.push(`hardware_hash.eq.${hardware_hash}`);\n      if (orParts.length > 1) query = query.or(orParts.join(','));\n      else if (device_fp)     query = query.eq('device_fp', device_fp);\n      else if (device_id)     query = query.eq('device_id', device_id);\n      else                    query = query.eq('hardware_hash', hardware_hash!);\n\n      const { data: banRows } = await query.limit(1);\n      if (banRows?.length) {\n        const b = banRows[0] as { ban_reason: string; banned_at: string };\n        return json({ banned: true, reason: b.ban_reason, banned_at: b.banned_at });\n      }\n      return json({ banned: false });\n    }\n\n    // ══ تسجيل جهاز في device_registry ════════════════════════════════\n    if (action === 'register_device') {\n      if (!userId) return json({ error: 'userId مطلوب' }, 400);\n      const { device_fp, device_id, hardware_hash, ip_address, device_model, platform, app_version } =\n        body as Record<string, string | undefined>;\n      await supabaseAdmin.from('device_registry').upsert({\n        user_id: userId, device_fp: device_fp ?? null, device_id: device_id ?? null,\n        hardware_hash: hardware_hash ?? null, ip_address: ip_address ?? null,\n        device_model: device_model ?? null, platform: platform ?? null,\n        app_version: app_version ?? null, last_seen_at: new Date().toISOString(),\n      }, { onConflict: 'user_id,device_fp', ignoreDuplicates: false }).catch(() => {});\n      return json({ success: true });\n    }\n\n    // ══ جلب قائمة الحظر ══════════════════════════════════════════════\n    if (action === 'get_device_bans') {\n      const { data: bans, error: bErr } = await supabaseAdmin\n        .from('device_bans').select('*').order('banned_at', { ascending: false }).limit(200);\n      if (bErr) return json({ error: bErr.message }, 500);\n      return json({ success: true, data: bans ?? [] });\n    }\n\n    return json({ error: `إجراء غير معروف: ${action}` }, 400);\n\n  } catch (err) {\n    return json({ error: String(err) }, 500);\n  }\n});\n"}]}
</action>

    21 
    22 function fmt(d?: string | null) {
    23   if (!d) return '—';
    24   try { return format(new Date(d), 'dd MMM yyyy HH:mm', { locale: ar }); }
    25   catch { return d; }
    26 }
    27 
    28 function shortFp(fp?: string | null) {
    29   if (!fp) return '—';
    30   return fp.length > 12 ? `${fp.slice(0, 6)}…${fp.slice(-6)}` : fp;

   189 // ── الصفحة الرئيسية ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   190 export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
   191   const navigate = useNavigate();
   192   const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'bans'>('duplicates');
   193 
   194   const [dupes, setDupes]       = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
   195   const [bans,  setBans]        = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
   196   const [loading, setLoading]   = useState(true);
   197   const [search, setSearch]     = useState('');
   198   const [filterBanned, setFilterBanned] = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');
   199 
   200   // حوار الحظر
   201   const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
   202   const [banNote, setBanNote]     = useState('');
   203   const [banning, setBanning]     = useState(false);
   204 
   205   // حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر
   206   const [unbanId, setUnbanId]     = useState<string | null>(null);
   207   const [unbanning, setUnbanning] = useState(false);
   208 
   209   const load = useCallback(async () => {
   210     setLoading(true);
   211     try {
   212       const [d, b] = await Promise.all([getDuplicateDevices(), getDeviceBans()]);
   213       if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
   214       else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
   215       if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
   216     } finally { setLoading(false); }
   217   }, []);
   218 
   219   useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);
   220 
   221   const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
   222     const q = search.toLowerCase();
   223     const matchQ = !q ||
   224       (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   225       (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   226       g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
   227       g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
   228     const matchFilter =
   229       filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
   230       filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned : !g.is_banned;
   231     return matchQ && matchFilter;
   232   });
   233 
   234   const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
   235     const q = search.toLowerCase();
   236     return !q ||
   237       (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   238       (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   239       b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   240       (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   241       (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
   242   });
   243 
   244   const handleBan = async () => {
   245     if (!banTarget) return;
   246     setBanning(true);
   247     const res = await banDevice({
   248       device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
   249       device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
   250       hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,
   251       ban_reason:           banNote.trim() || 'تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز',
   252       ban_type:             'both',
   253       notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
   254       associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
   255       associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,
   256     });
   257     setBanning(false);
   258     if (res.success) {
   259       toast.success('✅ تم حظر الجهاز نهائياً');
   260       setBanTarget(null);
   261       setBanNote('');
   262       await load();
   263     } else {
   264       toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');
   265     }
   266   };
   267 
   268   const handleUnban = async () => {
   269     if (!unbanId) return;
   270     setUnbanning(true);
   271     const res = await unbanDevice(unbanId);
   272     setUnbanning(false);
   273     if (res.success) {
   274       toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
   275       setUnbanId(null);
   276       await load();
   277     } else {
   278       toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');
   279     }
   280   };
   281 
   282   const activeBansCount = bans.filter(b => b.is_active).length;
   283 
   284   return (
   285     <AdminShell
   286       title="الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة"
   287       breadcrumbs={[
   288         { label: 'الإدارة', href: '/admin' },
   289         { label: 'الحسابات المكررة' },
   290       ]}
   291     >
   292       {/* إحصائيات سريعة */}
   293       <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 mb-4">
   294         {[
   295           { label: 'أجهزة مكررة', value: dupes.length, icon: Smartphone, color: 'text-warning' },
   296           { label: 'محظور منهم', value: dupes.filter(d => d.is_banned).length, icon: ShieldX, color: 'text-destructive' },
   297           { label: 'حظر نشط', value: activeBansCount, icon: Ban, color: 'text-destructive' },
   298         ].map(({ label, value, icon: Icon, color }) => (
   299           <div key={label} className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-3 text-center">
   300             <Icon className={`w-5 h-5 mx-auto mb-1 ${color}`} />
   301             <p className="text-lg font-bold tabular-nums">{loading ? '—' : value}</p>
   302             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{label}</p>
   303           </div>
   304         ))}
   305       </div>
   306 
   307       {/* شريط البحث + تحديث */}
   308       <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
   309         <div className="relative flex-1">
   310           <Search className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />

// ── الحسابات المحظورة (is_active = false) ─────────────────────────────────
export interface BannedAccount {
  id: string;
  username: string | null;
  email: string | null;
  full_name: string | null;
  phone: string | null;
  role: string;
  device_fp: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

/** جلب جميع الحسابات المحظورة (is_active = false) */
export async function getBannedAccounts(): Promise<{ data: BannedAccount[]; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('profiles')
    .select('id, username, email, full_name, phone, role, device_fp, created_at, updated_at')
    .eq('is_active', false)
    .order('updated_at', { ascending: false });
  if (error) return { data: [], error: error.message };
  return { data: (data ?? []) as BannedAccount[] };
}

function DuplicateGroupCard({
  group, onBan,
}: {
  group: DuplicateDeviceGroup;
  onBan: (g: DuplicateDeviceGroup) => void;
}) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);

          </p>
        </div>
        {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
